Local News Two

Four Kidnappers Executed 189

Three Criminals Compose Poems Separately 190

Ye Ruchun Firmly Maintains His Innocence

Rong Jiannan Believes He Deserves to Die

Zhu Rongsheng Misses His Elderly Mother

Wang Zhongmei Still Has Maxims

Ye Ruchun, a 37-year-old native of Yuyao, Zhejiang, residing at No. 15 Zhibu Road, Shanghai, owner of the Shanghai Gramophone Company, also worked as a special patrolman for the Public Concession Police. Due to suspicion of involvement in kidnapping, he was apprehended by Chief Inspector Lu Liankui, Inspector Liu Shaokui, and Detective Feng Zhiming of the General Inspectorate, along with his accomplices Rong Jiannan, Zhu Rongsheng, and Wang Zhongmei. All were handed over to the Special District Court for interrogation. It was revealed that Ye and his gang, on the evening of September 18th of last year, armed and organized, kidnapped Cai Fulin, a comprador of the British-American Tobacco Company, on Hart Road. Furthermore, in October of the same year, they robbed prostitutes Ye Feilong, Jia Baoyu, Miaofenglou, and Xiangfei of their belongings in rooms 44 of the Eastern Hotel and 314 of the New World Hotel. After repeated questioning and clarification, Ye, Rong, Zhu, and Wang were each sentenced to death. The sentences were reported to the Provincial Government for approval and execution. Yesterday morning marked the date of execution by firing squad. Ye Ruchun's elderly mother and wife, having received the news, arrived at the court grounds outside the Special Court around 7:00 AM, standing in anticipation. Around 8:00 AM, as Ye and the other three were escorted by the police, Ye's mother and others, upon seeing them, began to cry loudly, tears streaming down their faces, causing temporary disorder. After being dispersed by Chinese and Western police officers, order was restored. Subsequently, Judge Zhou Hanting presided over the Third Criminal Court, and Police Barrister Li Zhishan ordered the four defendants to be brought to the case one by one. According to Ye Ruchun's statement, he was 37 years old, from Yuyao, and previously worked with watches and clocks, and also as a special patrolman. He claimed complete ignorance of the alleged kidnapping case and insisted on his innocence, stating that if he knew anything about it, he would be willing to be subjected to lingering death and have his entire family shot. He requested justice. Judge Zhou repeatedly informed Ye that today was the execution date, and he could use this time to explain any last words to his family. However, Ye continued to shout and protest his innocence incessantly. Judge Zhou ordered him to be taken down. Following this, Rong Jiannan stated that he was 32 years old, from Wuxi, residing in Taide Lane. He said, "I am being executed today for kidnapping, and I do not feel wronged, but Ye Ruchun is completely innocent." Zhu Rongsheng stated that he was 29 years old, from Jiangyin, unemployed, and had no last words. His statement was the same as Rong's. Wang Zhongmei stated that he was 33 years old, from Jiangyin, and worked as a doctor. "Today, I represent all the criminals in prison to express my opinions to the judge. Most of the prisoners are currently suffering from illness. According to my experience as a doctor, this is undoubtedly due to starvation. Because the food in prison is insufficient, it fails to satisfy the prisoners' hunger. Kidnapping can be divided into three classes, and my involvement in kidnapping was not due to hunger or cold, nor was it for eating, drinking, or gambling, but purely for the country." He then began to rant about national affairs. His words were incoherent. Finally, he raised his voice and sang the Beijing opera "He Heavily Condemns Mao Yanshou." Judge Zhou ordered him to be taken down. Consequently, the Chinese and Western police officers, along with the entire case file and photos, escorted them onto a car and drove directly to the Caohejing execution ground. They notified the Local Court, which dispatched Prosecutor Wu Shixin as the execution officer, along with Clerk Qian Yinpei, Examiner Xuan Zhiming, and others. They also ordered Police Chief Xu Jinqing and Police Officer Chen Xihui to supervise the execution officers Wang Jianqing, Xue Bingzhang, Yin Daoxu, Zhu Wanyuan, Hu Xianglin, Zhang Chunsen, Zhou Qiwen, Zhu Baochang, Jiang Huanzhang, Li Jiajun, Chen Yinzhi, and more than ten others, who traveled to the execution ground by car. The judge then, along with Warden Dong Changmin, took their seats in the official position. Ye Ruchun was brought forward and stated, "I am 37 years old, from Yuyao, residing at No. 15 Zhibu Road. I have a mother, three wives, and sons at home. I want my family to teach my sons well. I am going to die, truly wronged." He had four lines of poetry to express to the heavens, a seven-character quatrain: "My body is killed, but my soul does not die, I go to the nine springs to chase your soul, There will be a day when retribution arrives, I am not afraid that your vicious fate is difficult to escape." He requested the clerk to record it, and tears streamed down his face. At this point, the official asked Rong Jiannan, "32 years old, from Wuxi, residing in Taide Lane, Hart Road. I have a mother and wife. The instigator of this case was Yang Yousheng. I also have a poem, please record it: "Living in this world, failing to recognize one's friends, has led to this. Today, I die without regret, but I pity Mr. Ye's deep innocence." Then, the official asked Zhu Rongsheng, "29 years old, from Jiangyin, residing at No. 11 Zhoujiaqiao. I have parents, a wife, and a child. I want my brother to be filial to my mother, do not worry about me." It was heard that Wang Zhongmei stated, "33 years old, from Dongtai, residing at No. 1155 Kade Lane, Xinzha Road. I have parents, a wife, and children. My will is to tell future generations not to be as absurd as I was. I completely fell into economic panic due to smoking and drinking, leading to my downfall and sacrificing my life. It was intentional, so I have a poem to advise a group of villains: "Evil is like a red flower, good is like a pine, the green pine is not as good-looking as the flower, one day when the frost falls, only the green pine is seen, not the flower." I also have a maxim to advise against smoking and drinking: "Smoking can ruin one's family," "Drinking can cause disaster." Alright, please execute me." The judge then ordered the execution. Police Chief Xu directed the police officers to execute the criminals by firing squad. The bodies were collected by the morgue to await identification by relatives.

Slave of a Vanquished Nation

Chinese Woman Forced into Marriage Due to Debt 191

Chen Ruiqing Plagued by Financial Difficulties

Daughter Subjected to Abuse by Indian Man

Indian Man Now Abandoning Daughter and Trying to Escape

Request for Strict Handling by the British Public Concession

Borrowing Money from an Indian: Chen Ruiqing, a native of Wuxian, Jiangsu, in his forties, runs the Wanyuanxiang Coffin Shop on North Chengdu Road in Shanghai. He has a daughter named Genfu, who is seventeen years old, fashionably dressed, and exceptionally beautiful. Chen loves her as the apple of his eye. However, Chen's shop is not doing well and often operates at a loss. He has no choice but to borrow from outside. He met an Indian man named Jagat Ram, who lives at No. 150 Mayback Road, already fifty years old. He possesses vast wealth but does not engage in production, relying on exorbitant interest rates to make a living. When lending money, regardless of the amount, he charges a flat monthly interest rate of 10% (i.e., one dime of interest per dollar borrowed per month). Chen, through various connections, became acquainted with Jagat. Learning that Jagat specialized in lending, he frequently borrowed money from him, accumulating debts of around 300 yuan, which he was unable to repay for a time.

Harassing His Cherished Daughter: After being introduced to Chen through friends and becoming more familiar with him due to their financial dealings, Jagat frequently visited Chen's home. He caught sight of Chen's daughter and was captivated by her beauty, harboring improper intentions. Therefore, he never mentioned collecting Chen's debts and often visited Chen's home at his leisure, deliberately acting lavishly, lingering, and reluctant to leave. Whenever he had the opportunity, he flirted with Genfu, offering her gifts that young women loved, flattering her with sweet words, and using all sorts of enticements. Genfu, being young and naive, was charmed by him, while Chen remained unaware.

Actually Marrying an Indian Man: Chen owed Jagat 300 yuan, which he had been unable to repay for a long time. By the end of last year, Jagat suddenly changed his usual amiable attitude and sternly demanded repayment, claiming that the principal and interest had reached over 600 yuan. If Chen did not repay, he would take him to court. He also said that he had a perfect solution for Chen's predicament. If Chen was willing to give his daughter in marriage to him, not only would the previous debts be completely canceled, but he would also give Chen another 400 yuan. Chen, plagued by financial difficulties, did not want his beloved daughter to be abused by this foreigner, but he had no other solution. Genfu, realizing that she had already lost her virginity to Jagat, did not object either. After several discussions, a marriage agreement was reached. They chose the 18th day of the lunar new year of this year to hold the wedding ceremony. An elderly husband and a young wife, with different nationalities, was truly an improper match.

Indian Man Secretly Planning to Return Home: After the marriage, their lives were relatively harmonious. Jagat gave Genfu one dollar every day to cover her small expenses, as usual. Recently, Genfu became three months pregnant. However, for some unknown reason, Jagat suddenly conceived the idea of returning home. He secretly moved all the household items out, abandoning Genfu. Yesterday, he secretly boarded the (Tevue) steamer to return home. Genfu received a tip from an Indian man (a friend of Jagat), and immediately rushed to the ship with her father, grabbing Jagat and crying hysterically. She accused Jagat of seducing and forcing her into marriage, and now abandoning her, and insisted on suing him in court. Chen also helped his daughter hold onto Jagat, refusing to let him go. Jagat struggled violently, punching Chen and injuring him, and tearing his trousers. Genfu's black Indian silk cheongsam was torn open on both sides, exposing her chest. Chen and his daughter were unable to succeed by force, and turned to the customs police station for help.

Truly Devoid of Conscience: Upon receiving the complaint, the police head dispatched Chinese detectives Sun Agui and Wu Wenqing, and Western detective Brett Sikes, who contacted the Hongkou Police Station. Detectives were dispatched to the ship to arrest Jagat and take him to the Hongkou Police Station to await interrogation by the British Public Concession. The head of the water patrol police station also ordered Chen to go to the hospital for a medical examination to serve as evidence of Jagat's assault. It was heard that Genfu stated in her statement to the police that she had been seduced by Jagat at the age of fifteen and forced into marriage this spring. Now, she is three months pregnant, but he treats her like a thorn in his side, moving out all the furniture and deliberately abandoning her. Even her beloved phonograph, which she had saved up for with her daily one-dollar allowance for groceries, was taken away, intending to return home and disappear. He is truly devoid of conscience. She will request the British Public Concession to severely punish him based on the above crimes.

Father and Son Commit Suicide One After the Other 192

Son Unable to Withstand Debt Pressure Commits Suicide

Father Unwilling to Live Due to Son's Death

Around 11:30 AM the day before yesterday, a case of father and son committing suicide occurred in the Zhoujiaqiao area in western Shanghai. The son, unable to withstand the pressure of debt, committed suicide by consuming opium. The father, grieving over his son's unnatural death, angrily committed suicide by stabbing himself with a knife. He was on the verge of death, causing a great commotion. Those who heard about it were saddened. The details are as follows:

Impoverished Family: Xia Yutian, a 51-year-old native of Tongzhou, currently resides at No. 22 of the Minsheng Yarn Factory Workers' Quarters in Zhoujiaqiao, western Shanghai. He only has one son, named Shaoqing, who is 22 years old. He works as a factory worker for a living, working diligently and frugally, and is loved by his father. Because the father is poor and elderly and unable to work, he relies entirely on his son for a living. Therefore, in recent years, Shaoqing has saved some money from his work, in addition to the living expenses of the father and son. Last summer, he married a woman named Zhang, from the same hometown, through a matchmaker. After the marriage, Shaoqing, bearing an even heavier burden, asked someone to introduce his wife, Zhang, to work at the Minsheng Yarn Factory to help with household expenses.

Committing Suicide by Smoking Opium: Around 12:00 AM the night before last, the Caojiadu Sixth District Police Station in western Shanghai received a report from women Xia Zhang, Zhang Weishen, and Jin Heshang, who brought Xia Caifu to the station, accusing Xia Caifu of forcing them to pay debts, leading to Mrs. Zhang's husband being forced to commit suicide by consuming opium. After separate inquiries by the district head, according to Xia Zhang's statement, her husband, Xia Shaoqing, had found it difficult to make ends meet this year due to the rising cost of living. He had borrowed 30 yuan from his paternal uncle, Xia Caifu, around May of the lunar calendar, agreeing to repay it in one month. Unexpectedly, as soon as the deadline arrived, the uncle repeatedly came to demand repayment and also asked Weng Yutian to collect the debt. Her husband, unable to find a solution, begged him to postpone it, but the uncle continued to press him. Her husband, forced to do so, conceived the idea of ending his life. Last night, after a slight argument with his uncle, he secretly consumed opium and committed suicide. He was sent to the Labor Hospital but could not be saved. She requested justice. According to Zhang Weishen, 30 years old, from Tongzhou, residing on Qimei Road, Xiangyan Bridge, Xia Shaoqing is my nephew-in-law. Her statement was the same as Xia Zhang's. According to Jin Heshang, 26 years old, residing on Broadway Road, he and the deceased Xia Shaoqing are friends. His statement was the same as above. According to the defendant, Xia Caifu, 39 years old, from Tongzhou, residing on Xiangyan Bridge, Shaoqing is his cousin. He had borrowed 30 yuan from me, and I did not force him excessively. I do not know the reason why he committed suicide by consuming opium.

Suiciding Out of Anger and Grief: Xia Yutian, the father of the deceased Xia Shaoqing, seeing his son die an unnatural death, immediately burst into tears, and his grief was overwhelming. Realizing that his son had died and there was no one to rely on, his livelihood was cut off. While his daughter-in-law and others were reporting the incident to the district office, he felt unwilling to live and took a sharp blade and stabbed himself forcefully three times in a row, causing blood to flow profusely and he collapsed to the ground. Neighbors, seeing the tragic scene, immediately rushed him to the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road. After examination by the doctor, there were three wounds on his testicles, and his scrotum was ruptured, causing a large amount of bleeding. He was dying. A report of the injury was submitted to the district office. His daughter-in-law, upon hearing this, was terrified and even more grief-stricken. Yesterday afternoon, it was reported that Xia Yutian had also died.

Taken to Court Together: After receiving the report, the Sixth District Head, believing that the case involved debt pressure leading to death, submitted a document yesterday morning to transfer the four original defendants to the Local Court for interrogation.

Zhu Shisheng's Sudden Death Case 193

Zhu Zhang Seems to Be Involved

Various Parties Say Her Reputation Is Terrible

Zhu Shisheng, a local native, 53 years old, owner of a local goods department store at No. 100 Yangshuo Road, had been widowed for many years and had three daughters. On the 24th of last month, his second daughter, named Simei, 26 years old, died of illness. On the same day, at noon, she was dressed for burial and a funeral was held. However, Zhu's second wife, Zhang, 28 years old, had a sudden argument with Zhu Shisheng around 6:00 PM because of Simei's death. Zhu suddenly fell to the ground and called for help, losing consciousness. Later, he was sent to Tongde Hospital at No. 1 Tongfu Road. Despite treatment by Dr. Qin, he died at 2:00 AM the next morning. His body was sent to the Philemon Road Morgue for examination. Zhang was taken to the police station by Detective Gui Shou of the Yangshupu Police Station, and the police chief ordered her to be transferred to the women's detention center to await trial.

Police Lawyer States the Case: Yesterday morning, Special Court Judge Xiao Xiefei of the First Special District specially opened the Third Criminal Court for trial. According to Police Barrister Li Zhishan's statement of the case, the police accused the defendant of the crime of injury resulting in death under Article 296 of the Criminal Law. Furthermore, it was found that the defendant's reputation was notoriously bad. At the time, the deceased's death was caused by injury to his testicles. Dr. Qin and many witnesses are present to testify. Dr. Qin's examination report was presented for inspection, and a request was made for a strict investigation.

Doctor Proves Blood Vessel Rupture: According to Dr. Qin Daoyuan's statement, he received a phone call around 10:00 PM that day and went to Zhu's home. Zhu Shisheng was already sleeping upstairs, unconscious. He was sent to my hospital. The cause of his illness was that he was old and weak, and his brain's blood vessels had ruptured. If the patient is frightened, angered, or hit by an object, his blood vessels will rupture. The lower part of his body was slightly swollen, but the scrotum was not broken. A little white discharge was visible in the glans, but it could not be determined whether it was indeed leukorrhea, nor could it be determined whether the testicles had been damaged. In short, the cause of death was blood vessel rupture. The defendant was present when Zhu Shisheng died and was detained. She also volunteered to go to court.

Eldest Daughter Sheds Tears While Testifying: Zhu Fuying, the eldest daughter of the deceased's first wife, 31 years old, married to Zhang Xinglin, stated that her stepmother and father were fighting, and she was out attending her sister Simei's funeral and did not witness it. When she returned, the crowd told her that her father had been beaten to death by his stepmother. She went upstairs to see her father, but he could not speak. In the past, her father and stepmother often quarreled because she had a lover outside. Her father repeatedly told her that he would definitely be harmed by her in the future and that she must seek justice for her father after his death. She shed tears as she spoke. The fifth daughter stated that she was 24 years old and lived in Yinxiang Port. She rushed there that day because of her sister Simei's funeral and saw many people at the door, saying that her father had been beaten by his stepmother and sent to Tongde Hospital. She went to visit him and saw that he could not speak.

Statements of Neighbors and Melon Sellers: According to witness Li Chunrong, who was a neighbor, Zhu Shisheng ran to the door and was chased out by the defendant, who pulled him into the shop and pushed him onto a rattan chair. Zhu cried out for help. Her husband and wife often quarreled, and it was heard that the defendant had an affair with someone outside. According to Yuan Abao, who was also a melon seller nearby, Zhu Shisheng was dragged into the shop by the defendant at the shop door and pushed into a chair, crying for help. Suddenly, he stopped speaking, as if he were dead. I persuaded the defendant not to beat him, but she said he was pretending to be dead. If he really died, she might buy four boards and six nails to make a coffin for him and told me to leave and not to meddle. According to Yao Fuqing, who was a worker in a nearby sock factory, as he passed by Zhu's shop, a woman told him that Zhu's boss had been brutally beaten by his wife and was about to die. According to Zhang Heshang, Zhu Shisheng was his uncle, and he did not see the defendant fighting, but he heard shouts for help. He went to see and saw him sitting in a chair.

Zhang Tries to Shirk Responsibility in Her Testimony: Zhang stated that she was married to the deceased and had been married for nineteen years and had seven pregnancies. They had always been on good terms. At the time, her son-in-law Zhang Xinglin invited people to come and beat me and trampled on her husband. I did not damage his testicles, but I did pull his arm. Her husband was addicted to alcohol and suffered from leukorrhea. Moreover, when her husband was dying, she did not run away from the hospital. After a while, police officers arrived to arrest her. The whole matter was that her son-in-law Zhang Xinglin wanted to plot against the family property. There were two Fang family contracts that he had borrowed. I wanted to rely on my husband for a living and would never do this. She also hired lawyers Lin Yinqing and others to defend her.

Debate Over, Date Set for Sentencing: Zhang Xinglin denied inviting the underworld people to beat the defendant. He was out attending his sister-in-law's funeral and returned to find that his father-in-law had been beaten by the defendant and was already upstairs. He immediately sent him to the hospital for treatment, but he could not speak. Zhao Di, the daughter of the defendant, stated that she was 14 years old and had also returned from attending her fourth sister's funeral. A moment later, underworld people arrived to beat her mother, and her father stepped forward to dissuade them and was pushed and fell down. Later, her mother helped her father into the shop. After the lawyers on both sides debated, Judge Xiao ordered Zhu Zhang to be remanded in custody and to set a date for sentencing.

Ball of Interest Money 194

Borrowing Two Dollars, Paying 20 Copper Coins in Interest Daily

Zhang Fugeng Unable to Repay Money, Uses Knife to Assault

Car driver Liu Wenluan, residing at No. 23 Xixiang Lane, Lafayette Road, French Concession, engages in lending money at exorbitant interest rates. Zhang Fugeng, a Suzhou native residing at No. 16 of the same lane, making a living by pulling a rickshaw, had borrowed two dollars from Liu and had to pay 20 copper coins in interest daily, which is commonly called "ball of interest money." At 9:30 PM the night before last, Liu demanded the interest money from Zhang but could not obtain it, causing a verbal dispute to arise. Zhang used a knife to slash Liu's legs twice, causing blood to flow profusely. Seeing that he had caused trouble, Zhang immediately abandoned the knife and fled, running to the intersection of Lafayette Road and Caishi Road. A French patrol police detective happened to be patrolling and saw it, and arrested Zhang along with his accomplice Shen Zaiqing and took them to the police station. Yesterday, they were taken to the Second Special District Court for questioning. First, the police's acting lawyer explained the case, and then the plaintiff recounted the circumstances of the stabbing. Zhang Fugeng stated that the plaintiff had first hit him, so he acted in a moment of desperation. Shen Zaiqing stated that he had been advising from the side and did not dare to assist in the assault. Judge Ge Zhitan reviewed the confession and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody to await a later trial.

Dr. Tang

Case of Accusation Against Zou Aizhen 195

Zou Aizhen Submits Petition for Transfer of Jurisdiction

Awaiting Investigation by the Local Court Before Ruling

Economic Doctor Tang Huixuan and Lawyer Yan Yang'an jointly submitted a petition to the Special District Court, requesting permission to divorce his wife, Zou Aizhen. The main points of the lawsuit have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Yi of the Special Court's Civil Division 10 summoned Tang Huixuan to court. Zou Aizhen did not appear, nor was she represented by a lawyer. Tang Huixuan first stated his age and place of origin. Judge Yang then inquired whether No. 48, Baoshan Li, Baoding Road was his residence or a temporary lodging. Tang replied, "I used to work in other places, and my address was not fixed. Now I have been living in Shanghai for a long time, and No. 48, Baoshan Li, is my residence. However, my parents live in my ancestral home in Guangxi." Judge Yang then stated, "Now Zou Aizhen has submitted a petition to this court, requesting a transfer of jurisdiction, because she does not live at No. 1296, Route Lafayette, but lives in the Chinese-controlled area of Ximen. Therefore, she requests that the case be transferred to the Local Court for trial." The petition was then given to lawyer Yuan to read. Lawyer Yuan immediately rose and said, "Zou Aizhen previously also filed a lawsuit in the Local Court seeking a divorce from Tang. Judge Tong, who was presiding over the case, wanted to transfer the case to your court because Tang had moved to the concession, but Zou was unwilling and withdrew the lawsuit. Zou's current action is illegal and should be rejected." Judge Yang then announced that the case would be adjourned and a ruling would be made after an investigation with the Shanghai Local Court.

A Section on Yesterday's Rain 196

Yesterday's weather was unusually hot, with the thermometer reaching 96 degrees. Around 2 p.m., dark clouds suddenly gathered, and a torrential downpour occurred in the Xiaonanmen area, accompanied by thunder. Immediately followed by a loud crash of lightning. Before long, the rain stopped and the sun came out. Some parts of Shanghai did not experience rain. During the heavy rain, the house of Zhang Zifeng, resident of No. 74, Yongxing Street, west of Xiaonanmen, was completely destroyed by lightning. For a while, the nearby residents crowded to watch, blocking the street. According to legend, a fox-like animal was struck by lightning, while others said a rat-like animal was struck, each person's account varied. However, the police officer stationed there stated that he only saw the roof being struck down and did not see any animal.

Shanghai Banking Association member National China Bank is a purely commercial savings bank run by banking experts, with particularly well-managed savings departments. It was the first to implement independent operations, transparent accounting, and unlimited liability for directors and managers. The use of savings is stable, and the protection is reliable. Staff services are sincere and friendly, procedures are quick, and interest rates are favorable. Accountants are also hired to check the accounts at any time, and the accounts of depositors are made public so that all can understand the department's business situation. Therefore, it has gained the trust of all sectors of society, and depositors are exceptionally enthusiastic.

The Da Ji Steamer Has Been Repaired 198

Today is the Test Run, Renamed Da Yu

The Dada Company's Da Ji steamer was damaged in the middle of the journey and towed back to Shanghai.

Page 16

Since the Rui Rong Shipyard undertook the repairs, everything above the main rudder has been rebuilt, and the passenger cabins have been reconstructed. The total cost of repairs is about 200,000 yuan. It has now been completed, and the ship has been renamed Da Yu. It is scheduled to leave the dock today for a test run. Once the speed is calibrated, it can be scheduled for regular service, and it is expected to resume service on the Tongyang line within two weeks.

Further News After Ye Sheng's Suicide 199

Regarding the suicide of the young man Ye Sheng, the court sent personnel to the coroner's office the day before yesterday to conduct an examination. Wu Laosan requested to waive the examination and, considering the past relationship, volunteered to take care of the funeral arrangements. The prosecutor approved it. Wu then bought a coffin and clothing, spending more than 200 yuan. It is found that the deceased Ye Sheng was indeed the grandson of the late Ye Chengzhong. He used to wander outside and did not engage in proper work, so he was expelled from the clan. At the beginning of this year, he met a woman named Wu Laosan, and they were deeply in love. They lived together on Longmen Road. At that time, Ye was in dire straits, and Wu Laosan provided him with food, clothing, and shelter. Later, Ye often went out to gamble, and his clothes were pawned. Ashamed to return home, he slept on the streets. When Wu Laosan found out, she tried to persuade him to no avail. Now his attitude had changed drastically, so he committed suicide by smoking opium.

Liang Yan Severing Ties 200

Liang Zhiyun, a native of Fenghua, former adjutant of the Review and Preparation Office of the Nanjing General Headquarters, currently residing at the corner of Yuanfang Road and Zhoujiazu, opposite the Lianhua Nunnery, was recently sued in the Mediation Court of the Special District Court by Yan Yiqing, a native of Ningbo, requesting confirmation of no marital status. The plaintiff's lawsuit briefly stated that the plaintiff is currently 35 years old, and the defendant, Liang Zhiyun, is currently 32 years old. The plaintiff used to live in Hong Kong and met the defendant when she was 25 years old. Later, they traveled to Shanghai together and then lived together in Shanghai. At that time, the plaintiff had considerable private savings, exceeding ten thousand taels of silver. After living with the defendant, it was gradually used up, and he had no occupation and idled his days. In recent years, because the plaintiff's private savings have been exhausted, he has been abusive and often threatened her, saying that he wanted to kill her with a gun. Leaving aside such remarks, the plaintiff and the defendant have lived together without a marriage contract, no betrothal gifts, no marriage certificate, no matchmaker, and no ceremony. The cohabitation is entirely without legal conditions, and of course, there is no marital status or marital relationship, like what is commonly called "concubinage." Since there is no marital status and no marital relationship, they are naturally not bound by each other in law, because the law does not protect or prohibit this kind of illegal union. Whether to unite or separate is entirely up to the free will of the individuals, and there is no need to go through legal procedures. The law is such, but the plaintiff and the defendant have lived together for a long time, and she is deeply afraid that outsiders will misunderstand the truth, mistakenly recognizing the plaintiff as the defendant's wife and mistakenly recognizing the defendant as the plaintiff's husband. In this way, the man will not be able to marry, and the woman will not be able to marry, and will be restrained by him. Now, the plaintiff is determined to break off cohabitation with the defendant, and in order to avoid misunderstandings and to lift all kinds of constraints, she specially submits a petition. Yesterday, the case was heard in the Ninth Mediation Court. Neither party appeared, and the plaintiff's lawyer, Yu Hualong, stated that the feelings between the two parties had already broken down, and it would be difficult to obtain happiness if they were forced to live together. The best plan now is to sever relations from now on, and each person will be responsible for their own debts. Men and women are free to marry and marry as they please. The defendant's lawyer agreed, and a mediation agreement was signed in court, formally severing relations. From then on, the couple separated like swallows.

Record of the Trial of Niu Lan and Others 201

According to the Guomin She, Niu Lan, director of the Eastern Department of the Third International, and his assistant Alis, were arrested by the Public Concession Police on June 15 in a secret Communist Party organ on Sichuan Road in this city, and more than 600 important pieces of evidence were seized. Among them, there were more than 100 documents concerning directing the Red Army in Jiangxi Province to resist the Central Government and providing economic assistance to the Communist Party throughout the country. At that time, it attracted the attention of the people of the whole country. The court postponed the trial until August 3 because it took a long time to organize the evidence. The following is a brief record of the trial. When the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court opened the trial of this case at 9 a.m. on that day, the observers included Mr. Zhang, representative of the Central Government, Zhan Jifeng, lawyer representing the Garrison Headquarters, and Lawyer Gan of the Police. Lawyer William, representing the defendant, was present. First, the judge inquired about the nationality, age, and name of the defendants Niu Lan and Alis. Then, the police lawyer reported the circumstances of the arrest and also stated that Niu and others should be extradited to mainland China for trial. Then Zhan Jifeng, the lawyer representing the Headquarters, rose and said that the case should be transferred to the inland government for trial. There are three preconditions: (1) Whether the defendant is a national of a country without treaty arrangements; (2) Where the criminal act took place; (3) Which judicial organ should handle the trial. On the first point, the defendant initially claimed to be a Belgian national, but after investigation, the defendant denied being a national of that country. Since the defendant cannot prove his nationality, he is a national of a country without treaty arrangements and should be subject to Chinese law. There is no doubt about this. On the second point, the defendant is an important person sent by the Third International to China to promote internal strife and engage in red-lining work. He is related to Zhu De and Mao Zedong, the leaders of the Red Bandits in Jiangxi, and Xiang Zhongfa, the Communist bandit recently arrested in Shanghai. The violent acts committed by these bandits all took place in the interior. Therefore, the defendant in this case should be extradited to be tried together. On the third point, the case committed by the defendant still violates the Emergency Criminal Law for Endangering the Republic of China. The Songhu Garrison Headquarters Military Law Review Office has the power to try the defendant. Also, according to Article 6 of the Agreement on the Recovery of Concession Courts, any criminal found in the Public Concession may be transferred to a government outside the concession after investigation by the court. Now, the two defendants are indeed criminals wanted by inland government according to law. Your court should assist and allow the investigators of our department to take the defendants back for interrogation. Then Zhang, the representative from the Central Government, explained the reasons and evidence for extraditing the criminals. (1) According to Gu Shunzhang, a member of the Central Committee of the Communist Party and director of the Special Affairs Department, who was arrested by the Wuhan Headquarters of the Commander-in-Chief in Hankou, the person in charge of the Third International in China was Mif. After he returned to his country, Niu Lan took over. According to Niu Lan's documents, the report to the Third International on Gu's arrest is very detailed. Based on this, it is sufficient to prove that Gu Shunzhang's confession is true, and at the same time, it can prove that Niu Lan is a major member of the Communist Party who endangers the Republic of China. (2) When Xiang Zhongfa, a member of the Central Committee of the Communist Party, was arrested by the Garrison Department in Shanghai, he confessed to Niu Lan. Recently, Niu Lan remitted a huge amount of one million to the Chinese Communist Party for activities. Niu Lan's documents also described Xiang Zhongfa in great detail, and there is evidence to check. Based on this, it can better prove that Niu Lan specializes in inciting internal strife in China. (3) Niu Lan's documents report the Third International's direction of the Jiangxi Red Army to resist the Central Army and the development of the Communist bandits in great detail. Based on this, it is sufficient to prove that Niu Lan is the chief culprit in instigating internal strife in China. The court must pay special attention to this. (4) Niu Lan's documents contain many reports on directing workers' riots throughout Shanghai and directing Communist Parties across the country to subvert the National Government. I hope that the court will transfer Niu Lan and others to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for trial according to military law. Then William, the defendant Niu Lan's lawyer, argued that, according to the Chinese Covenant Law, Niu Lan could not be tried by military law. Mr. Zhang, the representative from the Central Government, immediately stated that the Covenant Law should be followed, but the Niu Lan case is closely related to the Gu bandit arrested in Wuhan and the Xiang bandit arrested by the Songhu Garrison Headquarters. At the same time, it violates the martial law regulations in Jiangxi, Hubei, and Shanghai. It should be sanctioned by the Chinese authorities for endangering the Republic of China in order to comply with the law. At 10:30, the court ordered a change of date for another trial.

Military Operations to Suppress Shi Have Come to an End

The General Situation in North China Can Be Guaranteed and Established

Mayor Zhang received a telegram from Ma Fuxiang, Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission of the National Government, from Nanjing yesterday, saying, "To Mayor Zhang Yuejun of Shanghai: I received a telegram from Brother Weizhou to the East yesterday, saying that our Northern Route Army won a great victory, and all of Shi's rebels retreated in confusion to the north bank of the Hutuo River. The First and Second Army Corps are pursuing in separate directions. A detailed report is being sent to you. I think it is not fully recorded. According to a telegram from Secretary Xiao of our office, Shi Chen of our Northeast Army launched a full-line offensive. By 9 p.m., Shi's troops had completely collapsed under heavy casualties and fled to the north bank of the Hutuo River. The number of captured soldiers is about 15,000, and the number of dead and wounded is about 8,000 to 9,000. The Northeast Army sent five brigades of infantry and two brigades of cavalry, 20 airplanes, to follow and pursue. Shang Zhen has left Niangziguan to attack the rear of Shi's forces. The remaining enemies can be cleared up soon. The military operations to suppress Shi have come to an end, and the general situation in North China has been established, according to Hongkui's report, which is roughly the same. Shi's rebellion against the country has aroused the common indignation of heaven and man. With this great creation, it is the blessing of the country and the happiness of the people. Sincerely, Your Brother Ma Fuxiang, bowing Jiang Yin."

I also received a telegram from Brother Weizhou Jiangzi, saying, 'The Eastern telegram has been received. Our army captured many prisoners and seized countless spoils. Our First Army Corps has passed Dingzhou, and the vanguard of the army has arrived at Zhengding. From now on, those who spread rumors will have no words to fake, and the leisurely mouths will be silenced. Sincerely, Your Brother Ma Fuxiang, bowing Jiang Shen Yin."

Can a Hemp Rope Take a Life?

Iron Weapon Wound Behind the Head Suggests Something Else

A male corpse was found hanging near the back door of the hospital in Jinkang Lane, Xiaodongmen yesterday morning. The corpse was about thirty years old, wearing a black cloth short shirt, resembling a worker. He was hanging from only a hemp rope, obviously not hanging himself. The editor was also listed, there was blood behind his head, it was an iron weapon injury. After the Second Division of the First District found out, the circumstances were strange, ordered the local headman Pan Bingtang to report to the local court for verification. Appointed Inspector Wang and others to come to the scene to verify that he died from injury. The body was moved to that location. An order was issued to arrest the murderer.

Guang Shengtang Chinese Medicine Store is About to Open 210

Guang Shengtang Chinese Medicine Store, west of the Baxianqiao Small Vegetable Market, has been established for forty years. This time, the original site was rebuilt into a four-story, three-room new building, greatly expanded and renovated. It is now installing departments such as sliced medicines, pills and powders, ginseng and bird's nest, prescription delivery, decocting medicine for customers, mail order from other places, diagnosis and treatment, medical consultations, and drug research. Once all the equipment is ready, it will be opened.

Tianmu Weiya Dried Bamboo Shoots Arrive in Shanghai 211

Dried bamboo shoots are a specialty of Zhejiang, and those produced in Tianmu Mountain are especially famous. Mr. Zhou Yifan from Wulin specially invested a large amount of money to expand the area in Tianmu Mountain, using horticultural knowledge to plant a lot of fat bamboo. After harvesting the bamboo shoots, he used scientific methods to set up a factory to select and manufacture them. The quality is tender and the taste is fresh, and the price is low. A distribution office has been specially set up in Shanghai to serve those with the same preference.

Founding General Meeting of the Storytelling Industry Association 212

The Shanghai Storytelling Industry Association held its founding general meeting at the Oriental Storytelling Hall on Xizang Road yesterday morning at 10 a.m. More than 30 members attended, with a total of more than 40 representatives, as well as Hu Yuqi, representative of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and Xue Guangqian, representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Zhang Jihua, Yuan Mingjun, Zhan Wenxi, and Ni Yougen were elected as chairmen, and Yuan Minglin recorded. After the meeting began and the ceremony was performed, representatives from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce gave speeches successively. Then, the draft constitution and the election of executive and supervisory committee members were passed. As a result, Zhou Yingqing, Tang Zhaoxiong, Zhang Jihua, Yuan Mingjun, Yang Shenfu, Ni Yougen, Zhan Wenxi, Yuan Shunyuan, Xu Yaoting, and other nine people were elected as executive committee members. Zhao Jialin, Li Wenjun, Gu Guishan, and Xu Zihui and other four people were elected as alternate executive committee members, Chen Yunqu, Peng Huisheng, and Li Qixi and other three people were elected as supervisory committee members, and Gu Genfa was elected as alternate supervisory committee member. After the election, the entire group took a photo and adjourned the meeting.

News from Various Trade Unions 213

Bookbinding Industry Vocational Union Yesterday held its 19th board meeting, chaired by Chen Zhaoqing. The meeting was held as usual. (A) Reports (omitted). (B) Discussion. (1) The principals are still resisting the amendment of the treaty. What should be done? It was resolved that if the principals do not implement the treaty item by item, they should be reported to the higher authorities for the crime of disobedience and ordered to compensate for the losses. (2) How should we find a way to pay off the union's outstanding rent, the secretary's living expenses, and the loans? It was resolved that the dues would be collected at the end of the month. (3) The principal of Hexing Company resisted raising wages, causing labor-capital disputes. It was resolved that Chen Zhaoqing would be sent to negotiate with Ren Changfu. (4) The principal of Cao Yuji indiscriminately brought in apprentices, and recently added two new ones. How should we deal with this? It was resolved that the principal should dismiss the excess number of apprentices by a certain date and severely punish the introducer to warn others. (5) The 24 articles on the revised labor-capital treatment conditions of our union have now been printed. Should we distribute them to all workers and friends immediately? It was resolved to do so. (6) Should we send personnel to collect dues from the Western-style clothing aspect on the 5th and 6th? It was resolved that He Sheng'er, Shen Changjiang, Huang Songyue, and Chao Guosheng would be responsible. The rest is omitted.

Military Uniform Union Yesterday, the seventh board meeting resolved important cases. (1) In the future, the union's payment of funds of more than ten yuan must be approved by the board of directors. Each director and supervisor shall not make their own decisions. (2) The general affairs department must publicly inspect the income and expenditure items and the accumulated cash at each regular meeting. (3) When collecting dues, it must be signed and sealed by the executive director, supervisor, and the director of general affairs. (4) For workers who have not yet joined the union, the investigation department should persuade them to join the union. (5) A notice to all foremen to pay dues must be based on receipts. The union is not responsible for payments made without a formal receipt.

Tenth District Cotton Textile Union Yesterday held its third preparatory meeting, chaired by Fan Luquan. He reported that more than a thousand workers have joined the union, and the progress is very smooth. Next, important cases were resolved. (1) Reactionary slogans were found in the factory and turned over to the investigation department for secret investigation. (2) Yan Shude and Bao Yaozu were hired as assistant directors of the general affairs department. Yan Houzai and Guo Shaohua had documentary assistant directors, Wu Lanting was hired as a general affairs assistant director, and Sun Shouxiang and Bao Xuanlian were hired as directors of the guidance department. Shen Yaoming and Rong Bendao were hired as investigating directors. (3) The membership fee will be collected at the end of the month when wages are paid.

Weather Report 215

Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday: The Yangtze River basin will be hot and cloudy with thunderstorms. The East China Sea will have easterly winds, and the Yellow Sea will have undirected winds. The weather around the Ryukyu Islands is bad due to a hurricane moving slowly north or northeast-north. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 95.0 and the lowest was 77.2. On the same day last year, the highest was 94.1 and the lowest was 75.4.

Letter to the Editor 216

Dear Editor, I recently read a report in today's newspaper about the negotiations between the fire brigade and the telephone bureau. I was surprised to read that 30 or 40 members of our association surrounded the telephone bureau. Since our association was established last autumn and has been in operation for more than half a year, all expenses have been maintained by local gentry and businessmen who have borrowed and advanced money. Although the funding item has been approved by the municipal government and will be allocated monthly starting this year, it has not yet been received, so the economy is very stretched, resulting in several months of arrears in telephone bills. The bureau has not notified us recently and suddenly cut off the wires and stopped the call, resulting in the lack of news and the inability to rescue fire alarms, which has been criticized by the local area. Yesterday, due to the fire in Hongjili, Hongxing Road, the car arrived very late. The local people criticized us one after another. Our association has suffered injustice, so we went to the telephone to inquire about the reason for cutting the line and requested to restore the power. The surrounding situation may be a false rumor. I am deeply afraid of confusing the audience. Therefore, I hereby write to your newspaper for correction in order to show the reality, to the common friendship, Shanghai Zhabei District Fourth Section Fire Brigade, August 6.
